\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00019\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ header\ file\ provides\ Container-\/based\ versions\ of\ algorithmic\ functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00020\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ within\ the\ C++\ standard\ library.\ The\ following\ standard\ library\ sets\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00021\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ functions\ are\ covered\ within\ this\ file:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00022\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00023\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ *\ Algorithmic\ <iterator>\ functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00024\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ *\ Algorithmic\ <numeric>\ functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ *\ <algorithm>\ functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ standard\ library\ functions\ operate\ on\ iterator\ ranges;\ the\ functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ within\ this\ API\ operate\ on\ containers,\ though\ many\ return\ iterator\ ranges.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ All\ functions\ within\ this\ API\ are\ named\ with\ a\ \`{}c\_`\ prefix.\ Calls\ such\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}absl::c\_xx(container,\ ...)\ are\ equivalent\ to\ std::\ functions\ such\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}std::xx(std::begin(cont),\ std::end(cont),\ ...)`.\ Functions\ that\ act\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ iterators\ but\ not\ conceptually\ on\ iterator\ ranges\ (e.g.\ \`{}std::iter\_swap`)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ have\ no\ equivalent\ here.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ For\ template\ parameter\ and\ variable\ naming,\ \`{}C`\ indicates\ the\ container\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ which\ the\ function\ is\ applied,\ \`{}Pred`\ indicates\ the\ predicate\ object\ type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ to\ be\ used\ by\ the\ function\ and\ \`{}T`\ indicates\ the\ applicable\ element\ type.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00039\ }
